## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Envoy xDS v2 to v3 API Migration

## Your Task

Find all C++ source files in envoyproxy/envoy that implement both xDS v2 and v3 API handling: the versioned proto type conversion, the v2-to-v3 field renames (e.g., DiscoveryRequest), and the dual-version subscription handling in the ADS gRPC server.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the migration domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/envoy--v1.31.2, sg-evals/data-plane-api--84e84367, sg-evals/go-control-plane--71637ad6, sg-evals/grpc--957dba5e.

432026-03-08T21:21:39.286273agentmessage-
I am thinking...: Now I have a good understanding of the codebase. Let me summarize the key files that implement xDS v2 and v3 API handling in the Envoy repository:

1. **`source/common/config/type_to_endpoint.cc`** - This is the core file that maps xDS resource type URLs to versioned service methods. It explicitly mentions both v2 and v3 service names in comments (e.g., "envoy.api.v2.RouteDiscoveryService" and "envoy.service.route.v3.RouteDiscoveryService"). It builds a map from resource type URLs to v3 service methods (SotW, Delta, REST).

2. **`source/common/config/type_to_endpoint.h`** - Header for the above.

3. **`source/common/config/utility.h`** - Contains `checkTransportVersion()` which validates the transport API version (V2 vs V3) and emits deprecation warnings for V2.

4. **`source/common/config/utility.cc`** - Implementation of utility functions for xDS config handling.

5. **`source/common/config/subscription_factory_impl.cc`** - Factory that creates subscriptions based on config source type, calls `checkTransportVersion()`.

6. **`source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_mux_impl.cc`** - The legacy SotW gRPC mux implementation using `envoy::service::discovery::v3::DiscoveryRequest/Response`. The factory creates `GrpcMuxImpl` for SotW ADS.

7. **`source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/grpc_mux_impl.cc`** - The unified/new gRPC mux implementation (template-based) supporting both SotW and Delta. Instantiated with both `DeltaSubscriptionState` and `SotwSubscriptionState`.

8. **`source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/new_grpc_mux_impl.cc`** - The new delta gRPC mux implementation.

9. **`source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/sotw_subscription_state.cc`** - SotW subscription state handling, creates `envoy::service::discovery
... (truncated)

## Findings Summary

### Versioned Proto Type Conversion
| File | Role |
|------|------|
| `source/common/config/type_to_endpoint.cc` | Maps xDS resource type URLs → v3 gRPC service method descriptors. Comments explicitly reference both `envoy.api.v2.*` (v2) and `envoy.service.*.v3.*` (v3) service names. Exports `sotwGrpcMethod()`, `deltaGrpcMethod()`, `restMethod()`. |
| `source/common/config/api_version.h` | Defines `API_NO_BOOST` macro to suppress automatic v2→v3 proto boosting in specific files. |
| `source/common/config/protobuf_link_hacks.h` | Forces linker to include all v3 service proto descriptors (ADS, SDS, LDS, RDS, CDS, EDS, etc.). |
| `test/config/v2_link_hacks.h` | Forces linker to include v2 service proto descriptors for backward-compatibility in tests. |

### V2-to-V3 Field Renames / Transport Version Enforcement
| File | Role |
|------|------|
| `source/common/config/utility.h` | `checkTransportVersion<Proto>()` — rejects any `transport_api_version` that is not `AUTO` or `V3`, emitting: *"V2 xDS transport protocol version is deprecated…The v2 xDS major version has been removed."* |
| `source/common/config/subscription_factory_impl.cc` | Calls `Utility::checkTransportVersion()` before creating any subscription, enforcing v3-only transport. |
| `source/server/proto_descriptors.cc` | Validates at startup that all v3 proto method descriptors (`StreamAggregatedResources`, `DeltaAggregatedResources`, etc.) and type descriptors are present in the generated pool. |

Each package is independently versioned with a protobuf semantic\\\\n12: versioning scheme based on https://cloud.google.com/apis/design/versioning.\\\\n13: \\\\n14: The major version for a package is captured in its name (and directory structure). E.g. version 3\\\\n15: of the tracing API package is named `envoy.service.trace.v3` and its constituent protos are located\\\\n16: in `api/envoy/service/trace/v3`. Every protobuf must live directly in a versioned package namespace,\\\\n17: we do not allow subpackages such as `envoy.service.trace.v3.somethingelse`.\\\\n18: \\\"},{\\\"startLine\\\":1,\\\"endLine\\\":7,\\\"content\\\":\\\"1: # API versioning guidelines\\\\n2: \\\\n3: The Envoy project and [xDS working group](https://github.com/cncf/xds) take API stability and\\\\n4: versioning seriously. Below we articulate the API versioning guidelines that aim to deliver this\\\\n6: stability.\\\\n7: \\\"},{\\\"startLine\\\":75,\\\"endLine\\\":86,\\\"content\\\":\\\"75: Note that changes to default values for wrapped types, e.g. `google.protobuf.UInt32Value` are not\\\\n76: governed by the above policy. Any management server requiring stability across Envoy API or\\\\n77: implementations within a major version should set explicit values for these fields.\\\\n78: \\\\n79: # API lifecycle\\\\n80: \\\\n81: At one point, the Envoy project planned for regular major version updates to the xDS API in order to\\\\n82: remove technical debt. It explicitly mentions both v2 and v3 service names in comments (e.g., \"envoy.api.v2.RouteDiscoveryService\" and \"envoy.service.route.v3.RouteDiscoveryService\"). It builds a map from resource type URLs to v3 service methods (SotW, Delta, REST).\n\n2. **`source/common/config/type_to_endpoint.h`** - Header for the above.\n\n3. **`source/common/config/utility.h`** - Contains `checkTransportVersion()` which validates the transport API version (V2 vs V3) and emits deprecation warnings for V2.\n\n4. **`source/common/config/utility.cc`** - Implementation of utility functions for xDS config handling.\n\n5. **`source/common/config/subscription_factory_impl.cc`** - Factory that creates subscriptions based on config source type, calls `checkTransportVersion()`.\n\n6. **`source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_mux_impl.cc`** - The legacy SotW gRPC mux implementation using `envoy::service::discovery::v3::DiscoveryRequest/Response`. The factory creates `GrpcMuxImpl` for SotW ADS.\n\n7. **`source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/grpc_mux_impl.cc`** - The unified/new gRPC mux implementation (template-based) supporting both SotW and Delta. Instantiated with both `DeltaSubscriptionState` and `SotwSubscriptionState`.\n\n8. **`source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/new_grpc_mux_impl.cc`** - The new delta gRPC mux implementation.\n\n9. **`source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/sotw_subscription_state.cc`** - SotW subscription state handling, creates `envoy::service::discovery::v3::DiscoveryRequest`.\n\n10. **`source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/delta_subscription_state.cc`** - Delta subscription state handling.\n\n11. **`source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/delta_subscription_state.cc`** - Legacy delta subscription state.\n\n12. **`source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_subscription_factory.cc`** - Factory that creates gRPC subscriptions, selects between unified and legacy mux implementations.\n\n13. **`source/common/config/protobuf_link_hacks.h`** - Forces linking of v3 service protos.\n\n14. **`test/config/v2_link_hacks.h`** - Forces linking of v2 service protos (for testing).\n\n15. **`source/server/proto_descriptors.cc`** - Validates that v3 proto descriptors are available.\n\n16. **`source/common/config/api_version.h`** - Defines `API_NO_BOOST` macro for preventing API boosting.\n\nThe key aspects of the v2-to-v3 migration:\n- `type_to_endpoint.cc` explicitly references both v2 and v3 service names in comments\n- `utility.h` has `checkTransportVersion()` that rejects V2 transport\n- The gRPC mux implementations use v3 proto types exclusively\n- `v2_link_hacks.h` forces linking of v2 protos for backward compatibility in tests\n- `protobuf_link_hacks.h` forces linking of v3 protos for production\n\nThe \"dual-version subscription handling in the ADS gRPC server\" is implemented in:\n- `grpc_mux_impl.cc` (legacy SotW ADS)\n- `xds_mux/grpc_mux_impl.cc` (unified SotW+Delta ADS)\n- `new_grpc_mux_impl.cc` (new delta ADS)\n- `grpc_subscription_factory.cc` (selects between unified and legacy based on runtime feature flag)\n\nThe versioned proto type conversion is handled in:\n- `type_to_endpoint.cc` -
